_ngcontent-jyi-c1="" _nghost-jyi-c6="" class="ng-tns-c6-944 ng-tns-c1-943 ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><div _ngcontent-jyi-c6="" class="blz-page-content-view__content ng-trigger ng-trigger-loadingFade"><blz-page-view-title _ngcontent-jyi-c6="" class="ng-tns-c6-944" _nghost-jyi-c17=""><!----><blz-page-title _ngcontent-jyi-c17="" class="blz-page-title ng-star-inserted" style=""><!----><!----><h1 class="blz-page-title__headline ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><!----> World of Warcraft Profile APIs <!----><!----></h1><!----><!----><!----><!----><div class="blz-page-title__actions"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></div><!----></blz-page-title></blz-page-view-title><blz-page-view-description _ngcontent-jyi-c6="" class="ng-tns-c6-944" _nghost-jyi-c27="" class="ng-star-inserted" style=""><!----><!----><!----><blz-page-section _ngcontent-jyi-c27="" class="blz-page-section blz-page-section--extra-spacing ng-star-inserted"><div _ngcontent-jyi-c27="" apphandlecontentclicks="" class="document-content document-headers"><p>The World of Warcraft profile APIs listed below encompass profile game data. For more information about profile game data, see <a href="/documentation/world-of-warcraft/guides/namespaces">World of Warcraft Namespaces</a>.</p>
<h2 id="host-names">Host Names</h2>
<p>For all regions except China, the API host name follows the format <code>{region}.api.blizzard.com</code>, where <strong>{region}</strong> is one of <strong>us</strong> | <strong>eu</strong> | <strong>kr</strong> | <strong>tw</strong>. For China, the host name is <code>gateway.battlenet.com.cn</code>. For more information, see <a href="/documentation/guides/regionality-and-apis">Regionality and APIs</a>.</p>


<h2 id="namespaces">Namespaces</h2>
<p>The World of Warcraft profile APIs </p><p>require a namespace as part of every request. Each endpoint below lists the correct namespace to use as a parameter. A namespace can be submitted as a header (<code>Battlenet-Namespace: {namespace}</code>) or as a query parameter (<code>?namespace={namespace}</code>). For more information, see <a href="/documentation/world-of-warcraft/guides/namespaces">World of Warcraft Namespaces</a>.</p>
<p></p>
<h2 id="apis">APIs</h2>
<p>World of Warcraft supports the following profile APIs. For information about using the APIs, see <a href="/documentation/guides/getting-started">Getting Started</a>.</p>

                  /profile/user/wow
                </div></div></div></div></mat-panel-title></span><!----><span class="mat-expansion-indicator ng-tns-c44-946 ng-trigger ng-trigger-indicatorRotate ng-star-inserted" style="transform: rotate(180deg);"></span></mat-expansion-panel-header><div class="mat-expansion-panel-content ng-trigger ng-trigger-bodyExpansion" role="region" aria-labelledby="mat-expansion-panel-header-162" id="cdk-accordion-child-162" style="visibility: visible;"><div class="mat-expansion-panel-body"><app-api-reference-method _ngcontent-jyi-c42="" _nghost-jyi-c45=""><form _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="api-reference-method ng-untouched ng-pristine ng-valid" novalidate=""><!----><section _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" appdocumentlinks="" class="method-description ng-star-inserted" style=""><p>Returns a profile summary for an account.<br><br>Because this endpoint provides data about the current logged-in user's World of Warcraft account, it requires an access token with the <strong>wow.profile</strong> scope acquired via the <a href="/documentation/guides/using-oauth/authorization-code-flow">Authorization Code Flow</a>.</p>

                  /profile/wow/character/{realmSlug}/{characterName}/status
                </div></div></div></div></mat-panel-title></span><!----><span class="mat-expansion-indicator ng-tns-c44-1137 ng-trigger ng-trigger-indicatorRotate ng-star-inserted" style="transform: rotate(180deg);"></span></mat-expansion-panel-header><div class="mat-expansion-panel-content ng-trigger ng-trigger-bodyExpansion" role="region" aria-labelledby="mat-expansion-panel-header-192" id="cdk-accordion-child-192" style="visibility: visible;"><div class="mat-expansion-panel-body"><app-api-reference-method _ngcontent-jyi-c42="" _nghost-jyi-c45=""><form _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="api-reference-method ng-untouched ng-pristine ng-valid" novalidate=""><!----><section _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" appdocumentlinks="" class="method-description ng-star-inserted" style=""><p>Returns the status and a unique ID for a character. A client should delete information about a character from their application if any of the following conditions occur:</p><ul><li>an HTTP 404 Not Found error is returned</li><li>the is_valid value is false</li><li>the returned character ID doesn't match the previously recorded value for the character</li></ul>The following example illustrates how to use this endpoint:<ol><li>A client requests and stores information about a character, including its unique character ID and the timestamp of the request.</li><li>After 30 days, the client makes a request to the status endpoint to verify if the character information is still valid.</li><li>If character cannot be found, is not valid, or the characters IDs do not match, the client removes the information from their application.</li><li>If the character is valid and the character IDs match, the client retains the data for another 30 days.</li></ol><p></p>
</section><!----><table _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="ng-star-inserted" style=""><thead _ngcontent-jyi-c45=""><tr _ngcontent-jyi-c45=""><th _ngcontent-jyi-c45="">Parameter</th><th _ngcontent-jyi-c45="">Type</th><th _ngcontent-jyi-c45=""><!----> Value <!----></th><th _ngcontent-jyi-c45="">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody _ngcontent-jyi-c45=""><!----><tr _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="ng-star-inserted"><td _ngcontent-jyi-c45=""> :region </td><td _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="parameter-type"> string <!----><div _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="parameter-required blz-text-accent ng-star-inserted"> Required </div></td><td _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="parameter-value"><!----><mat-form-field _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="mat-form-field ng-tns-c47-1143 mat-primary mat-form-field-type-mat-input mat-form-field-appearance-legacy mat-form-field-can-float mat-form-field-should-float mat-form-field-hide-placeholder ng-untouched ng-pristine ng-valid ng-star-inserted"><div class="mat-form-field-wrapper"><div class="mat-form-field-flex"><!----><!----><div class="mat-form-field-infix"><input _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" class="mat-input-element mat-form-field-autofill-control cdk-text-field-autofill-monitored ng-untouched ng-pristine ng-valid" matinput="" id="mat-input-746" aria-invalid="false" aria-required="false"><span class="mat-form-field-label-wrapper"><!----></span></div><!----></div><!----><div class="mat-form-field-underline ng-tns-c47-1143 ng-star-inserted"><span class="mat-form-field-ripple"></span></div><div class="mat-form-field-subscript-wrapper"><!----><!----><div class="mat-form-field-hint-wrapper ng-tns-c47-1143 ng-trigger ng-trigger-transitionMessages ng-star-inserted" style="opacity: 1; transform: translateY(0%);"><!----><div class="mat-form-field-hint-spacer"></div></div></div></div></mat-form-field><!----></td><td _ngcontent-jyi-c45=""><!----><section _ngcontent-jyi-c45="" appdocumentlinks="" class="ng-star-inserted"><p>The region of the data to retrieve.</p>

<!-- battlenet nav -->
<script>
  (function () {
    document.addEventListener('blz-nav:cms-loaded', (event) => {
      const [accountDropdown] = event?.detail?.cmsContent?.filter((el) => el?.id === 'account')
      accountDropdown.querySelector('#blz-nav-battlenet').icon = "battlenet"
      accountDropdown.querySelector('#blz-nav-log-out').href = "/login/logout?ref=%2F"
  })})();
</script>
